if (!is_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') != '1e4e27fccc581253521d23eb4d3d4a8c71871810') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== '1e4e27fccc581253521d23eb4d3d4a8c71871810') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== '56ef410f8211f9bb54bdcae06ee219177b826348') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== '1e4e27fccc581253521d23eb4d3d4a8c71871810') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != '8e76b1798f81d1147d29059b9c5fe26c9da89ab9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '8e76b1798f81d1147d29059b9c5fe26c9da89ab9') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '6675d5dfd78df7d803047c53dcb12efba2425d30') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '8e76b1798f81d1147d29059b9c5fe26c9da89ab9') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') != '34d566232f1ab732db86a6cb1726beaca804a369') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '34d566232f1ab732db86a6cb1726beaca804a369') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== 'b72a6e0df7cf804b341efad346a38d36f4d3f924') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '34d566232f1ab732db86a6cb1726beaca804a369') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
		}
	}
}

	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('R1BMLTIuMS1vbmx5ICAgICAgICAgIAp0d2JzL2Jvb3RzdHJhcCAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgIHY1LjEuMyAgICAgICAgICAgICAgTUlUICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAKdHdlZWIvdGlueW1jZS1pMThuICAgICAgICAgICAgICAyLjAuMyAgICAgICAgICAgICAg'));
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('IE1JVCAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgCnZha2F0YS9qc3RyZWUgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgMy4zLjEyICAgICAgICAgICAgICBNSVQgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgIAo='));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (!is_file('vendor/licenses')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/licenses');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('vendor/licenses')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/licenses');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/licenses') != '33a8da38faa85800e535a063a5bb1aaf9ebe229f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/licenses');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/licenses', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/licenses');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== '33a8da38faa85800e535a063a5bb1aaf9ebe229f') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== 'c7522ef60a740b1c74cac7c1df29463c62634b86') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/licenses');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/licenses');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/licenses')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/licenses', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== '33a8da38faa85800e535a063a5bb1aaf9ebe229f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/licenses');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 690\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 690') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
